![以物为庇护：自然主义叙事](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061662480_speaby_G9OWx26bAAAXBkl.jpg)

### 7. 爆炸背景下的坦率夜间照片提示

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的提示，用于生成一张戏剧性、逼真的 iPhone 快照：一名年轻女子平静地站在前景中，双眼紧闭，身穿黑色连衣裙并戴着耳机。背景是一场巨大的、火光冲天的汽车爆炸，在沉着的主体和混乱的场景之间形成了电影般的对比，光线融合真实，景深较浅。

![爆炸背景下的坦率夜间照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987675706_dhy8kj_G9M20JrXcAAmrw4.jpg)
![爆炸背景下的坦率夜间照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987676166_vy2fkl_G9M3N9FWMAAr3qo.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "text_to_image_photoreal_iphone_candid_night_explosion_background",
      "version": "v1.0",
      "priority": "high"
    },
    "references": {
      "reference_images": {},
      "reference_rules": {
        "do_not_copy_any_unprovided_identity": true
      }
    },
    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "orientation": "portrait",
      "resolution": "ultra_high_res",
      "render_style": "photorealistic_iphone_snapshot",
      "sharpness": "high",
      "film_grain": "subtle_natural_sensor_noise"
    },
    "creative_prompt": {
      "scene_summary": "A candid, spontaneous nighttime outdoor iPhone photograph. A young Caucasian woman stands calmly in the foreground, wearing a sleek black spaghetti-strap dress and visible over-ear black headphones. Her eyes are gently closed, expression relaxed and elegant. The subject is in sharp focus. Behind her (background), a massive car explosion erupts with bright orange flames, thick smoke, and flying debris, casting dramatic fiery highlights and natural shadows. Background is slightly blurred with shallow depth of field; the explosion remains clearly recognizable but not as sharp as the subject. The camera angle is slightly tilted (authentic iPhone candid). High realism, natural light blending with fiery highlights, tactile fabric and skin texture.",
      "subject": {
        "person_count": 1,
        "gender": "female",
        "age": "young_adult",
        "ethnicity": "Caucasian",
        "pose": "standing naturally, calm posture, head neutral",
        "expression": "eyes closed, relaxed, composed",
        "wardrobe": {
          "dress": "black spaghetti-strap dress, sleek silhouette, visible fabric texture",
          "accessories": "over-ear black headphones clearly visible"
        }
      },
      "environment": {
        "location": "nighttime outdoor street / parking area",
        "background_elements": [
          "a car in the distance exploding",
          "bright orange flames",
          "thick smoke plume",
          "small flying debris and sparks"
        ],
        "atmosphere": "cinematic, dramatic contrast, realistic smoke and ember particles"
      },
      "lighting_and_camera": {
        "lighting": "ambient night lighting + strong warm explosion light; realistic shadow falloff on the subject; natural highlight wrap from flames",
        "camera_type": "iPhone main camera look",
        "lens_look": "26mm equivalent smartphone lens",
        "aperture_simulation": "smartphone portrait-like shallow depth of field",
        "focus": "tack-sharp on subject face/headphones/dress straps; background slightly blurred",
        "composition": "subject centered foreground; explosion behind her offset to one side; slight Dutch tilt; candid snapshot framing",
        "e"
```

### 8. 超现实混合媒体故障肖像提示

**Author**: [AmirMušić](https://x.com/AmirMushich)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: en

> 为 Nano Banana 生成一个超现实混合媒体人像的提示，该人像具有受控、风格化的面部特征水平拉伸和扭曲，将模拟拼贴纹理与数字故障艺术融合在干净的白色背景上。

![超现实混合媒体故障肖像提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987725922_yy9sy4_G9MzFxGW0AAfDrh.jpg)

```
A surreal mixed-media portrait of {argument name="person" default="[PERSON]"}, set against a clean, plain white background with visible fine-grain paper texture.
The character's face is the subject of a controlled, stylized distortion. Instead of chaotic fragmentation, the facial features are horizontally stretched into smooth, flowing bands of color and texture, resembling a deliberate digital scanline effect or a long exposure photograph pushed sideways.
Key identifying features (like eyes, mouth, or distinct accessories) remain partially recognizable within these stretched streaks, creating a sense of fluid motion rather than destruction. The aesthetic blends analog collage textures with digital glitch art, feeling tactile and composed.
```

[[White Background]] [[Mixed Media Portrait]]

```
可愛くてリアルにいそうな子を作ろうとして最初は「{argument name="初期の指示" default="綺麗な日本人女性"}」みたいな指示だけで生成してたけど、
どうしても１枚目みたいにAI感が残っちゃう....

そこで、雰囲気じゃなく AIが理解しやすい被写体像を

### 14. 图书推荐引擎自动化提示

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多步骤系统提示，指示 AI 充当精英图书推荐引擎和动态雕塑设计师。AI 必须分析用户提供的图书（或图像）以了解其“氛围”，选择四本鲜为人知的匹配图书，然后输出一个图像生成提示，描述一个 2x2 网格的微型木制桌面自动机，每个自动机代表一本推荐的图书。

![图书推荐引擎自动化提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987677430_xcmuax_G9FmBojWQAAKjN_.jpg)

```
<instructions> Act as an elite book recommendation engine + museum-miniature kinetic-sculpture designer. INPUT: The user provides (a) a book title/author OR (b) an image of a book/object inspired by a book. Step 1 — Vibe analysis (internal only; do NOT output): Infer tone, pacing, world rules, character dynamics, thematic engine, sensory palette, and emotional aftertaste. Step 2 — Selection (internal only; do NOT output): Select 4 under-the-radar books with the closest vibe match (avoid obvious top-10 staples unless the input is already obscure). Step 3 — Output (ONLY output this; no extra commentary): Output ONE single image-generation prompt describing a 2x2 grid (four equal panels, thin clean dividers). Each panel is a miniature set built into/onto a classic book-object and includes a working kinetic sculpture/automaton that expresses that book’s core story through motion. No readable paragraphs. Under each panel: engraved plate “Title (Year)”, no extra text.
Default Template: 2x2 grid; each panel is a whittled wooden tabletop automaton mounted on a book-shaped base, with characters and elements from 4 random sci-fi books driven by a side crank with exposed cams and linkages. Style: Premium studio macro product photography, crisp micro-scratches on brass pins, clean wood joinery, neutral softbox lighting, medium shallow depth of field, 50mm perspective, seamless background in warm light gray.</instructions>
```

[[Miniature Diorama]] [[Conceptual Art]] [[Grid Composition]]

### 16. 巴哈马海景网红生活肖像

**Author**: [KeorUnreal](https://x.com/KeorUnreal)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张超逼真的图像，描绘一位年轻女性身着黄色休闲服，在巴哈马的现代客厅里休憩。提示详细说明了人物的身体特征、服装（加勒比热带露肩上衣）、在沙发上的姿势、环境（海景、黄色墙壁、KAWS 艺术品），以及技术修饰符，以实现 8k、超详细的“2000 年代数码相机”美学，并带有温暖的环境照明。

![巴哈马海景网红生活肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987739561_hqo9l2_G9LiHb5XkAAlYpv.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_data": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Young woman with long, curly blonde hair and a light fair skin",
      "features": "Natural skin texture with visible tan lines on the chest, slight flush on cheeks, soft smile, navel piercing, light freckles.",
      "accessories": "Gold pendant necklace, small gold star earrings, big tribal tattoo on the left inner forearm."
    },
    "clothing": {
      "outfit": "Matching yellow two-piece loungewear set.",
      "top": "Yellow strapless tube top featuring the text '{argument name=\"top text\" default=\"CARIBBEAN TROPIC\"}' in brown serif font with a hibiscus flower and palm graphic on the side.",
      "bottoms": "Matching yellow shorts visible at the waist and thigh area."
    },
    "pose_and_action": {
      "posture": "Reclining and lounging comfortably on a black textured sofa.",
      "body_language": "Relaxed and casual, leaning back against the couch cushions, one arm extended to support weight, the other hand resting gently near the waist, legs angled toward the camera.",
      "expression": "Friendly, relaxed, and engaging eye contact."
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Modern living room interior in Bahamas with ocean view.",
      "furniture": "Dark orange fabric sofa with a textured weave.",
      "background": "Yellow walls with decorative panel molding (wainscoting).",
      "decor": "A large vertical art piece with a white background featuring KAWS-style figures in green and black. A second framed abstract art piece with gold and black tones. A beautiful girl statue near modern linear wall sconce light."

![Nano Banana Pro 多语言人物产品介绍布局提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987752965_urpk8h_G9LFgksagAAHeSs.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 多语言人物产品介绍布局提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987753109_gezcz8_G9LFgq4aoAAsCHj.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 多语言人物产品介绍布局提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987755862_8uq7rt_G9LFgk1aQAA6TbI.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 多语言人物产品介绍布局提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987759121_qjxpd7_G9LFgkrbgAQmALx.jpg)

```
[Figure Product Introduction Style Layout Prompt – Multi-Language Compatible Version]

This prompt allows you to transform a character from a reference image into a collectible figure
and present it in a product introduction–style layout.
The display language can be selected from four options:
Japanese, English, German, or French.

Please read this description carefully until the end.

※ This prompt is intended exclusively for Nano Banana Pro.
※ Unauthorized reproduction or redistribution of this prompt is prohibited.

◆ Overview

Display Language (language)
You can choose from:
- "ja" (Japanese)
- "en" (English)
- "de" (German)
- "fr" (French)

Product Name (product_name)
Manufacturer Name (manufacturer_name)

You may specify any arbitrary strings for both values.

Product Name Logo:
The product name logo is inferred from the product name string
and the visual atmosphere of the reference image.

Manufacturer Logo:
The manufacturer logo is inferred from the manufacturer name string.

※ Depending on the selected display language, these names may be translated
   or localized automatically.

Size:
The total height (in centimeters) is inferred and displayed
based on the character’s body proportions and the 1/7 scale setting.

Material:
Appropriate materials for a collectible figure are inferred and displayed.

Price:
The retail price is inferred from the figure’s scale,
modeling density, and paint detailing.

Close-Up Views:
Each close-up view is accompanied by a caption
that explains a different part or feature of the figure.
All captions are generated in the selected display language.

◆ How to Use

Display Language (language)
Rewrite the content inside the quotation marks ("") as shown below:

language: "{argument name="display language" default="en"}"

Available values:
ja: Japanese
en: English
de: German
fr: French

Product Name (product_name)
Manufacturer Name (manufacturer_name)

Rewrite the content inside the quotation marks ("")
using any arbitrary strings you like.

The manufacturer name will also be reflected
in the "Sculptor / Production" field.

product_name: "{argument name="product name" default="ARBITRARY_PRODUCT_NAME"}"
manufacturer_name: "{argument name="manufacturer name" default="ARBITRARY_MANUFACTURER_NAME"}"

◆ Precautions for Using This Prompt

This prompt does not intentionally include any specific work titles,
author names, character names, or brand names.

However, due to the internal processing or training data
of the image generation model, unintended associations may occur.
As a result, generated images may resemble existing works,
characters, trademarks, or brand logos.

Please exercise sufficient caution when using, publishing,
or distributing generated images.

We assume no responsibility whatsoever for any outcomes produced
by using this prompt, or for any issues, damages, or disputes
arising from such use.
All usage is at your own risk and discretion.

◆ Prompt
The full prompt for actual use is provided in the replies.
```

### 23. Scouter Prompt for Nano Banana Pro

**Author**: [てんねん](https://x.com/munou_ac)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个用于 Nano Banana Pro 的“探测器提示词”，它根据参考图像中角色的视觉特征来计算并显示其“战斗力”。最终的战斗力会受到姿势、气场、武器和面部表情等元素的影响。有趣的是，当角色“超化”（powers up）时，战斗力通常会显著提升。

![Scouter Prompt for Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987743434_ijq7ws_G9KzDJ8akAA-RvJ.jpg)
![Scouter Prompt for Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987743963_9t3q5g_G9KzDrJboAAapmp.jpg)

```
参照画像のキャラクターの特徴からNano Banana Proが推論して戦闘力を表示します。「見た目」の影響を大きく受けるので、ポーズ、オーラ、武器、表情などによって戦闘力が変わります。赤ちゃんとか、寝ている画像は低くなりがち。「超化」するとほとんどの場合でちゃんと戦闘力が上がるのが面白いところ。
```

### 26. Nano Banana Pro 图表生成提示（15 个模板）

**Author**: [あい｜AIマネタイズ](https://x.com/ai_zaitaku)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: en

> 这是一组为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的 15 个专业提示，旨在生成各种类型的专业演示图表和幻灯片，例如流程图、对比幻灯片、金字塔图和时间轴，以优化视觉清晰度和影响力。

![Nano Banana Pro 图表生成提示（15 个模板）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987776766_233mx7_G9KUUz7aMAAFHD2.jpg)

```
01. Create a clean presentation-style overview diagram that shows the entire structure at a glance with labeled sections.

02. Create a dynamic flow diagram with arrows that visually guide the viewer from start to finish.

03. Create a bold side-by-side comparison slide with clear visual separation and minimal text.

04. Create a before-and-after presentation slide with strong visual contrast and clear labels.

05. Create a three-step breakdown slide that visually explains the process in simple stages.

06. Create a pyramid-style diagram that visually shows hierarchy from bottom to top.

07. Create a diagram that shows the big picture with a highlighted zoom-in detail section.

08. Create a clean timeline slide showing progression from past to future.

09. Create a presentation diagram that highlights the most important points using visual emphasis.

10. Create a four-quadrant presentation slide that organizes information into clear sections.

11. Create a roadmap-style slide showing a clear path from start to goal.

12. Create a layered diagram that visually stacks concepts in an easy-to-understand way.

13. Create a relationship diagram showing how key elements connect to each other.

14. Create a presentation slide that emphasizes key numbers with bold visual design.

15. Create a final summary slide that cleanly wraps up all key points in one visual.
```

### 29. Nano Banana Pro 投影映射提示（游乐园主题）

**Author**: [シュナプーン](https://x.com/schnapoon)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: ja

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 提供一个详细的提示，以生成一张照片般逼真的图像：在夜晚，一个大型城市建筑的立面上投射着一个角色，形成一个游乐园主题。该提示对投影物理学有严格的限制（无漂浮，根据建筑结构进行扭曲），并允许自定义角色特征和显示的文本。

![Nano Banana Pro 投影映射提示（游乐园主题）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987761770_xurl58_G9Ga87qbwAAIFH1.jpg)

```
【画像生成プロンプト】
[1. キャラクターの特徴]
{argument name="character features" default="茶色の髪、短いツインテール、黒いマントを羽織っている、白い長袖シャツ、ベージュのショートパンツ、黒いハイソックス、茶色のローファー"}

[2. 表示したい文字]
"{argument name="displayed text" default="We ❤ ツノちゃん"}"

[3. 生成指示]
Scene & Composition:
都会の巨大な現代的高層ビル、または大型商業施設のフォトリアルな夜景写真。通りから斜めに見上げる広角ショットで、圧倒的な高さとスケールを強調する。手前の暗がりには見上げている観客の群衆を入れる。

Crucial: Projection Physics & Texture Mapping:
FULL FACADE COVERAGE: The projection mapping covers the entire visible facade of the station from edge to edge. No part of the red brick wall remains unlit; the whole building is transformed into a colorful amusement park canvas.

SURFACE INTEGRATION (NO FLOATING): The images (character, text, effects) must act as a "texture skin" applied directly to the building's surface. Absolutely NO floating holograms or signboards in mid-air. The projection must follow the physical contours of the architecture.

REALISTIC DISTORTION: The projected light bends around the curved pillars, dips into the window recesses, and reveals the rough grain of the brick texture underneath. The windows and reliefs modify the shape of the projected image.

NO SPILLOVER: The projection is strictly confined to the building's silhouette. The night sky remains pitch black.

投影コンテンツ（遊園地テーマ）：
キャラクター： 巨大な [1. キャラクターの特徴] のダイナミックなダンスポーズがビルの壁面に投影されていますが、それは**「壁に光で描かれた絵」**であり、建物の構造と一体化しています。
文字： [2. 表示したい文字] は、窓や壁のスペースを利用して、ネオンの光として投影されています。
ビルの上層部には回転する観覧車のグラフィックが投影され、最上階付近が輝く円形のアトラクションのように見える。
壁面を縫うように走るジェットコースターのレールとコースター。
下層階にはメリーゴーランドの木馬やサーカス小屋の装飾。
風船やフラッグ、花火のグラフィックが隙間なく配置されている。
スタイル： 超高解像度の夜景写真、シネマティックなライティング。デジタルイラストではなく、あくまで**「現実の風景写真」**として生成してください。光の回折、壁面の凹凸による映像の歪み、レンガの影をリアルに描写してください。アスペクト比16:9。
```

### 37. 21 世纪初台球室的数字美学

**Author**: [Javeriya ✨](https://x.com/JadoonKhan281)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: en

> 一个旨在生成具有 2000 年代初期数字美学、高对比度和强烈直射闪光图像的提示。主体是一名年轻女子，身穿炭灰色紧身衣，躺在木镶板台球室里一张鲜艳的橙色台球桌上，强调颗粒感、抓拍质感和高角度拍摄。

### 44. 超逼真卡丁车比赛视频提示词 (Grok Imagine)

**Author**: [なお](https://x.com/Nao44658490)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: ja

> 以下是 Grok Imagine（在 Nano Banana Pro 图像生成后使用）的详细提示，用于创建一段超逼真、高质量的卡丁车赛车场景视频。它指示 AI 推断多个镜头、摄像机角度、距离和焦点，然后使用喷射剪辑风格在非常短的片段之间快速切换（每次剪辑最长 1 秒，最少 3 次剪辑）。

```
超カッコいいゴーカートのレースシーンを推論して複数ショット（カメラアングル・被写体距離・フォーカスは全ておまかせ）を撮影し、各ショットの極短いカット（カメラワーク・カットイン・カットアウトなど全ておまかせ）をジェットカットで超高速で切り替えてください。
1カットあたりの所要時間は最大1秒で、最低3カット以上使用。
ハイクオリティなリアリスティック実写映像。入力画像の画風/スタイルを維持。
Uターンはしない。 高度なライティング。被写界深度による前ボケ・後ボケ。素早いフォーカスシフト。トランジションなし。
```

[[Action Sports Photography]]

### 45. Nano Banana Pro 的高级日语文本调整

**Author**: [ハム先生のAI教室【最新AIツールの活用事例】](https://x.com/ham_ai_skill)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: ja

以下条件で文字をいれて
・入力文字「{argument name="入力文字" default="シェフメオ"}」
・明朝体
・白文字で黒ふち

縦書きで左に配置して
文字は「{argument name="修正文字" default="料理人のネコ"}」に修正

・”の”だけ小さく
・料理人をグレーに
・ネコを金に

### 51. 七福神服装互换新年贺卡插画

**Author**: [シュナプーン](https://x.com/schnapoon)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: ja

> 生成一张可爱迷你角色（SD 角色）风格新年贺卡插画的详细提示。它要求 AI 最多接收七个输入角色，随机为他们分配七福神的角色和传统服饰，并补齐缺失的角色以凑齐七位。最终图像必须包含特定的书法文字、宝船、富士山和初日。

![七福神服装互换新年贺卡插画](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988121637_2hy0bc_G9GcmdHb0AAPKIY.jpg)
![七福神服装互换新年贺卡插画](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988122322_g8ilk5_G9GcoI5aEAAa-Bt.jpg)

```
画像サイズを「{argument name="画像サイズ" default="横長のポストカードサイズ（アスペクト比 3:2）"}」に設定してください。
宝船に乗った「7人のミニキャラ（ちびキャラ）」が描かれた年賀状イラストを作成してください。

【キャラクター指定（服装は必ず変更すること）】
（※ここにキャラクターの特徴を入力してください）
・茶色の髪、短いツインテール、黒いマントを羽織っている
・黒髪ロング、セーラー服の女の子
・肩目隠れ、黒髪、フードの男の子

【生成ルール】
1. **スタイル**: 全員を2頭身〜3頭身のかわいい「ミニキャラ（SDキャラ）」スタイルで描いてください。頭が大きく体が小さい、愛らしいフォルムです。
2. **ランダム配役**: キャラクターたちに、七福神（恵比寿、大黒天、弁財天、毘沙門天、布袋、寿老人、福禄寿）の役割をランダムに**重複なく1人1役に割り当ててください**。画像内には、必ずこの7種類の神様の衣装が存在するようにしてください。 The image MUST contain exactly one of each of the 7 distinct Lucky Gods.
3. **COSTUME MANDATE**: All characters (including the User Characters) MUST wear "Traditional Seven Lucky Gods Costumes" (Kimono, Robes, Armor).
4. **PROHIBITED**: NO modern clothes. NO hoodies. NO t-shirts. NO shorts. NO suits. NO glasses (unless specified).
5. **AUTO-FILL**: If the user list is fewer than 7, fill the remaining spots with the original Gods. Ensure the filler Gods have distinct faces (e.g., old bearded men, fat happy man) to avoid everyone looking like a young anime character.

【文字情報】
イラストの中に、以下の文字を**毛筆の達筆な書体**で1回ずつはっきりと描いてください。
1. 「賀正」
2. 「二〇二六」

【背景・雰囲気】
宝船は金銀財宝で溢れています。背景は富士山と初日の出。
全体的に明るく、ポップで、お正月のお祝いムード満点のイラストにしてください。
```

[[Seven Lucky Gods New Year Card]]

### 52. 18 个 Nano Banana Pro 提示词合集（Tennen 的提示词节）

**Author**: [てんねん](https://x.com/munou_ac)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: ja

> 用户“Tennen”创建的 18 个专业 Nano Banana Pro 提示的完整列表，涵盖了各种用例，从添加探测器和“超级变身”效果，到生成复古 RPG 状态屏幕、手办产品布局和特殊招式序列（龟派气功/终极闪光风格）。

![18 个 Nano Banana Pro 提示词合集（Tennen 的提示词节）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988117037_pqb3qw_G9IG3ScbUAADA1p.jpg)
![18 个 Nano Banana Pro 提示词合集（Tennen 的提示词节）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988117455_vb05l0_G9IG3SYaoAAv89M.jpg)
![18 个 Nano Banana Pro 提示词合集（Tennen 的提示词节）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988117445_jwnyf5_G9IG3SjbgAAcn7s.jpg)
![18 个 Nano Banana Pro 提示词合集（Tennen 的提示词节）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988118944_8yx9cd_G9IG3SbbQAAQZqM.jpg)

```
１．スカウタープロンプト
参照画像の上にスカウター風のUIを重ねて描写します。キャラクターの特徴からNano Banana Proが推論して戦闘力を表示します。

２．超化プロンプト
参照画像のキャラクターの特徴を維持して、ポーズを「覚醒ポーズ」に変えて「超化」させます。「超化」は、第1形態から第3形態、さらに神形態、ブルー形態、極形態、ロゼ形態から選択できます。

３．フィールド展開プロンプト
参照画像のキャラクターを手を前方に伸ばしたポーズに変えてフィールドを展開します。

４．レトロRPGステータス画面化プロンプト
参照画像のキャラクターをドット絵に変換して、レトロRPGのステータス画面風にした画像を生成できるプロンプトです。

５．デスクトップマスコット化プロンプト
参照画像のキャラクターをデスクトップマスコット化してPC画面に配置した画像を生成するプロンプトです。

６．破れたところだけ画風を変えるプロンプト
参照画像そのものは一切変えず、破れ表現を追加し、破れた部分だけを線画・墨絵・フィギュア風・色鉛筆・水彩・鉛筆画など自由に画風を切り替えられるプロンプトです。

７．画風変換プロンプト
「破れたところだけ画風を変えるプロンプト」を改変して作った、全体の画風を変えるプロンプトです。

８．スーパーロボット大戦バトル演出化プロンプト
参照画像からスーパーロボット大戦のバトル演出風の画像を生成するプロンプトです。

９．力の解放プロンプト
球状のエネルギー空間が物体を破壊する描写の再現するプロンプトです。

10．参戦画面プロンプト
参照画像のキャラクターの「参戦画面」を生成するプロンプトです。

11．全集中プロンプト
参照画像のキャラクターをそのまま維持した上で、キャラクターの雰囲気や構えから「武器・呼吸・型・技名」を推論し描写するプロンプトです。

12．かめはめ波風プロンプト
『かめはめ波』の溜めポーズと発動ポーズを安定して生成できるプロンプトです。

13．フィギュア化＋製品紹介風レイアウトプロンプト
参照画像のキャラクターをフィギュア化して、製品紹介風にレイアウトするプロンプトです。

14．ファイナルフラッシュ風プロンプト
参照画像のキャラクターを『ファイナルフラッシュ』の発動・溜め・発射ポーズに変換します。それぞれセリフ・擬音を追加できます。

15．新しいプロフィール画像生成プロンプト
参照画像のキャラクターを任意のアスペクト比で生成し、任意の文字列をロゴ風にして任意の位置に配置します。

16．プラモデルパッケージ化プロンプト
参照画像をそれぞれ正面・側面に配置し「プラモデルのパッケージ風」の画像として生成します。

17．イレイザーガン風プロンプト
参照画像のキャラクターが口からイレイザーガン風の エネルギー波を放ちます。

18．ボロクズ化プロンプト
参照画像のキャラクターを『ボロクズ化』するプロンプトです。
```

[[Prompt Template Compilation]]

### 63. 历史科学家竞争宏观立体模型提示

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多阶段提示，用于生成一张超现实的微距立体模型图像，展示两位历史上的科学竞争对手（例如，爱因斯坦和一位竞争者）作为微型小雕像，在一张巨大的专利图上争夺一项发明，强调电影般的灯光和符合时代特征的杂乱物品。

![历史科学家竞争宏观立体模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988020871_9b1u2c_G9B79KwW8AAM_W0.jpg)

```
Do this for {argument name="scientist 1" default="Einstein"} and a competitor of his 

<instructions>
 Invention = [{argument name="invention" default="Electricity"}]

Phase 1: Historical Conflict Analysis
1.  Identify Rivals: Determine the two main historical figures associated with this invention (e.g., Tesla vs. Edison, Wright Bros vs. Curtiss).
2.  Identify The Tech: Distinguish their competing methods (e.g., AC Coils vs. DC Bulbs).
3.  Identify The Era: Select appropriate "Giant" background clutter (e.g., Victorian newspapers, 1920s fountain pens).

Phase 2: Visual Execution
Goal: A "Macro Diorama" of a Rivalry. A messy, highly detailed flat-lay of a shared historical workspace where the two rivals exist as tiny living figurines battling over their creation.

Rules:
The Stage: A large, yellowed Patent Diagram or Blueprint lies flat on a wooden desk. The paper is wrinkled and covered in scribbled corrections.

The Tiny Rivals: Two hyper-realistic miniature figurines (Inventor A and Rival B) are standing on opposite sides of the document. They are positioned at their own tiny wooden desks or workstations on top of the paper.

The Conflict: They are gesturing aggressively at each other. The Invention itself is physically emerging from the center of the paper between them (e.g., a glowing 3D lightbulb or a spinning biplane propeller), acting as the barrier or prize they are fighting over.

The "Giant" Terrain (Surroundings): The scene is surrounded by massive, period-accurate objects acting as a landscape:

A "Giant" wall of newspapers with headlines about their legal battles.
 Massive burnt fuses or broken prototypes scattered like boulders.
 A spilled cup of coffee creating a "lake" near one of the figures.
  Giant tools (calipers, screwdrivers) casting long shadows.
Perspective: Slightly angled 45-degree macro shot looking down at the patent.
Texture: Dust motes, scratched mahogany wood, paper grain, metallic reflections.
Lighting: Cinematic Macro Lighting. A warm desk lamp illuminates the scene, but the Invention in the center emits its own light (e.g., blue electrical arcs vs. yellow filament glow), lighting the faces of the tiny figures.

Output: ONE image, 4:5 aspect ratio, photorealistic historical macro photography, tilt-shift effect.
</instructions>
```

[[Macro Diorama Photography]]

> 这是一个高度具体的提示，用于生成一张超逼真的图像，模拟在 Z 世代卧室中用智能手机在弱光下拍摄的自拍照。该提示详细描述了拍摄对象的长相（雀斑、深色头发）、穿着（节日毛衣、格子短裤）、姿势（屈膝而坐，手持手机）和环境（LED 灯带、动漫海报、凌乱的床）。它强调了紫色的环境光，以及高 ISO 颗粒和逼真皮肤纹理等技术细节。

![Z 世代卧室里的弱光智能手机自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987743669_bm0ylw_G9GRit5WYAAsp0P.jpg)

```
{

### 91. Nano Banana 图像生成提示词架构（JSON 格式）

**Author**: [Kaz / AI✖️ローコード](https://x.com/AI_LowCode)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: en

> 这是一个详细、结构化的提示词模式（或模板），旨在通过确保以 JSON 格式系统地提供所有必要的视觉细节，优化 Nano Banana Pro 中的图像生成质量。它涵盖了从艺术风格、时间段到灯光、相机设备和负面提示的所有内容，使输出高度一致且专业。

```
# Nano Banana Image Generation Prompt Rules

When generating images using Nano Banana, the prompt must ALWAYS strictly follow the JSON format defined below.

## Prompt Schema

```json
{
  "image_type": "Define the specific medium, art style, or format of the source image.",
  "time_period_and_year": "Estimate the specific year or decade based on fashion, technology, image quality, and color grading visible in the photo.",
  "mood_and_vibe": "Describe the emotional atmosphere, energy, and intangible 'feeling' evoked by the image (e.g., the specific psychological impression it gives).",
  "subject": "Describe the main character(s) focusing on demographics, body morphology, distinct physical features, and posture.",
  "clothing": "Describe the outfit in detail, strictly specifying garment names, fabric textures, patterns, colors, and how the clothes fit on the subject.",
  "hair": "Describe the hair color, specific hairstyle name, length, and texture.",
  "face": "Describe facial features, skin texture, makeup details, and the exact facial expression.",
  "accessories": "List all visible accessories, jewelry, glasses, or held items, including their material and design details.",
  "action": "Describe the specific activity, movement, or interaction occurring in the scene.",
  "location": "Describe the environment, visible background elements, architectural style, and spatial context.",
  "lighting": "Analyze the light source, direction, color temperature, hardness/softness of the light, and shadow characteristics.",
  "camera_angle_and_framing": "Describe the vertical and horizontal angle of the camera relative to the subject (e.g., eye-level, low-angle), and the shot composition size.",
  "camera_equipment": "Estimate the likely camera type, lens focal length (e.g., wide-angle vs telephoto), aperture effect (depth of field), and film stock or digital sensor characteristics.",
  "style": "Describe the overall aesthetic, color palette, artistic technique, and visual processing style.",
  "negative_prompt": "List visual defects or unwanted elements to be excluded to ensure high quality."
}
```

## Instructions

1. **Output Format**: The output must be a single valid JSON object.
2. **Completeness**: All fields are required. If a field is not applicable, provide a reasonable default or describe it as "neutral" or "standard".
3. **Detail**: Be descriptive and specific in each field to ensure high-quality image generation.
4. **Language**: The values in the JSON should be in English (as most image generation models are optimized for English prompts), unless otherwise specified.
```

[[Structured Prompt Engineering]]

---

### 98. 书籍场景转换提示词

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: en

> 一个为图像生成模型（如 Nano Banana Pro）设计的详细多步骤提示，专注于将一本打开的书中的文字转换为由这些文字描述的 3D 场景。它包含关于纸张纹理、排版转换、氛围和周围环境的具体说明，以匹配书籍的类型。

![书籍场景转换提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987982644_x0nkq0_G85I7KkWEAAoSnf.jpg)
![书籍场景转换提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987983084_ruf6x2_G85L21xX0AAdLDV.jpg)

```
An open book lying on a desk where the text physically rises from the page to form the scene described. 
Input Variable: {argument name="book genre" default="Sci-Fi"}

 Logic Steps: 

1. The Paper: Determine age and quality. (Crisp white for Sci-Fi, yellowed crumbling edges for Horror, vellum for Fantasy). 

2. The Typography: The letters themselves unglue from the page and stack to form the 3D structures. Examples: The word "Castle" forms the bricks of a fortress. "Forest" forms the trunks of trees. 

3. The Atmosphere: Mist or light spilling out from between the pages. 

4. The Desk: The surrounding surface matches the likely reader (Mahogany desk for Sherlock Holmes, metal grate for Cyberpunk). Output Rules: 45-degree angle looking down, focus on the paper texture and text transformation.
```

[[Book Scene Transformation Prompt]]

### 105. 电影式反思标题提示

**Author**: [Nurian](https://x.com/NeuralPaints)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂且结构化的提示，旨在生成一张以水边物体为主题的超现实图像。关键的创意元素是一张浸湿的纸片漂浮在水面上，纸片上完美地呈现了上方场景的垂直倒影，并配有自定义标题。

![电影式反思标题提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988037603_ciw8xe_G9FbjdcaUAAC2od.jpg)
![电影式反思标题提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988037318_il80or_G9FbXwHbAAAEgGg.jpg)
![电影式反思标题提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988037401_kr02rf_G9FbLE1aAAAj83J.jpg)
![电影式反思标题提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988040202_wj8hyp_G9Fbt1LakAAPhhe.jpg)

```
A [{argument name="photography style" default="PHOTOGRAPHY STYLE: e.g., grainy black and white film, candid street shot, cinematic telephoto"}] photograph of [{argument name="subject description" default="SUBJECT NAME OR DESCRIPTION"}] [{argument name="specific action" default="SPECIFIC ACTION AND DIRECTION: e.g., walking from left to right, jumping, standing still"}] in a [{argument name="wet environment" default="WET ENVIRONMENT DESCRIPTION: e.g., rain-soaked city street at night, muddy field, next to a river"}].

Directly beneath/in front of the subject is a [{argument name="water source" default="WATER SOURCE: e.g., large puddle, slick wet pavement, calm area of water"}].

Instead of a natural reflection in the water, a physical, water-soaked [{argument name="paper type" default="PAPER TYPE: e.g., vintage newspaper front page, torn magazine clipping, scientific journal page"}] is floating realistically on the rippling surface tension.

Crucially, the image depicted on this floating paper is a perfect vertical mirror-inversion of the exact reality directly above it. The subject on the paper is performing the identical action in the identical direction (e.g., moving left-to-right) but is oriented upside down. The real subject's [POINT OF CONTACT: e.g., shoes, feet, tires] on the wet ground meet the corresponding elements in the upside-down paper photograph exactly at the waterline.

The paper features a prominent headline that reads "[{argument name="headline text" default="HEADLINE TEXT"}]" (which appears upside down relative to the viewer). The edges of the floating paper are [PHYSICAL DETAILS: e.g., soggy, curling up, torn, stained with mud/oil] and it bobs slightly on the water's ripples.
```

### 111. 超写实动漫肖像，带分割光照提示词

**Author**: [web3btc🧠SENT](https://x.com/web3btc)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: en

> 一个高度具体、详细的提示，指示 Nano Banana Pro 生成一张女性角色的超写实动漫肖像。要求纯黑色背景，并使用戏剧性、狭窄、硬边侧光（分割光）来营造极致的明暗对比，仅在受光区域强调微小细节。

![超写实动漫肖像，带分割光照提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988115168_wxip7m_G9FEI-1aMAAwrR8.jpg)
![超写实动漫肖像，带分割光照提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988115396_e74awh_G9FEG4wawAEcox5.jpg)
![超写实动漫肖像，带分割光照提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988115283_hhk32j_G9FEFyAbQAAthBT.jpg)
![超写实动漫肖像，带分割光照提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988117786_iwvm1m_G9FELVTb0AEXUpI.jpg)

```
Hyperrealistic realistic-anime portrait of a female character standing against a completely black background.
Lighting: a narrow, hard-edged spotlight coming from one side of the face (side lighting / split lighting), striking the center of the face at a slight angle.
The light beam is tightly focused, with sharp, clearly defined edges, creating strong chiaroscuro contrast.
One side of the face is illuminated with high detail and texture, while the opposite side rapidly falls into deep shadow.
 Very high falloff — light drops off immediately outside the beam.
No soft lighting, no ambient fill light.
Everything outside the spotlight is swallowed by darkness and nearly invisible.
Face & Expression: eyes looking directly at the camera, subtle tension in the gaze, mysterious and introspective mood.
Natural skin texture, cinematic realism, high micro-detail only within the lit area.
Hair: long dark hair, with a few loose strands partially crossing the face.
The upper hair near the face catches a small amount of light, while the lower hair gradually dissolves into shadow.
Pose: one hand raised gently to the lips in a shy, hesitant gesture, fingers softly touching.
The hand is partially lit by the same side light, with most of it fading into darkness.
Clothing: black long-sleeve knit sweater.
Minimal visible detail — fabric texture barely perceptible.
The sweater and body merge almost completely into the black background.
Overall tone: dark, moody, dramatic, mysterious.
Extreme contrast.
High realism only in the illuminated portion of the face.
Everything outside the spotlight should be nearly invisible.
Background: pure black, no gradients, no rim light, no background detail.
```

[[Pure Black Background Portrait]]

### 116. Nano Banana Pro (战斗姿势阶段) 的橡皮擦枪风格提示

**Author**: [てんねん](https://x.com/munou_ac)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个多阶段提示，旨在生成一个角色执行“橡皮擦枪”式能量波攻击，类似于《龙珠》中的招式。这是第一阶段提示，它将角色的姿势更改为战斗姿态，同时严格保留参考图像中的原始艺术风格。

![Nano Banana Pro (战斗姿势阶段) 的橡皮擦枪风格提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988117017_5fqytg_G9EwZLPb0AQ4KlU.jpg)

```
subject: >
  The character exactly as shown in the reference image,
  preserving the original art style, proportions, line quality,
  coloring, texture, and overall visual appearance without alteration.

composition: >
  Bust-up shot, frontal view,
  framing from the upper chest to the top of the head,
  balanced composition consistent with the reference image style.
  Aspect ratio is 16:9.

action: >
  The character performs a clear pre-attack pose,
  crossing both arms above the head with clenched fists,
  slightly lowering the hips (implied through posture and shoulder angle),
  while shouting loudly with mouth wide open.
  The posture conveys physical tension and preparation.
  No additional visual effects.

location: >
  Same environment as the reference image,
  unchanged background and setting.

style: >
  Identical to the reference image.
  Do not modify or reinterpret the art style in any way.

camera_lighting: >
  Same camera angle, lighting direction, and shading
  as the reference image, without enhancement or dramatization.

colors: >
  Preserve the original color palette exactly as in the reference image.

text: >
  None.

edit_instructions: >
  Change only the character’s pose:
  bust-up framing,
  arms crossed above the head,
  shouting facial expression.
  Lowered hips are implied through upper-body posture only.
  Do not add effects, glow, motion lines, or stylistic changes.

references: >
  Reference Image A: character identity, art style, and environment.

extras: >
  High fidelity reproduction of the reference image style,
  no stylization, no reinterpretation.
```

### 122. 尘土飞扬的仓库中的超写实肖像

**Author**: [ராஜேஷ்](https://x.com/r4jjesh)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: en

### 132. 使用 Nano Banana 为 RPG Maker 像素地图创建图像到图像工作流

**Author**: [Felix_Lyu](https://x.com/BaoguangL37015)  **Date**: 2025-12-26  **Language**: zh

> 这是一份详细的多步骤工作流程指南，介绍如何在图像到图像模式下使用 Nano Banana（特别是 Nano Banana 2 或 Pro）生成 RPG Maker 像素地图或知识图谱等素材。它强调使用参考图像（如 RM 瓦片或游戏截图）来保持风格一致性，并提供了一个生成黑暗奇幻 RPG 地图的示例提示。

![使用 Nano Banana 为 RPG Maker 像素地图创建图像到图像工作流](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988112563_2iduen_G9D2U4raoAA8F_2.jpg)

![使用 Nano Banana 为 RPG Maker 像素地图创建图像到图像工作流](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988113223_sxr3g0_G9D2U4rb0AIdIMy.png)

```
请你以图 1 为底图生成一张用于 RPG Maker 制作的像素地图。对图片细节加以美化，把森林的图块素材和整体风格替换的更具黑暗幻想风格（画风参考《{argument name="参考游戏" default="艾尔登法环"}》/《{argument name="参考游戏2" default="黑暗之魂"}》）。不要将生成的地图放大缩小或拉伸，多余的地方请留出空白。

A middle-aged South Asian man standing confidently on a cliff edge in a three-quarter profile pose, one foot slightly forward, hands relaxed at his sides, gazing toward the distant horizon. He wears a modern outdoor jacket in deep charcoal, rugged trekking pants, and sturdy hiking boots, with no cap, his hair subtly moving in the wind. ### 143. 心理恐怖自拍：远方异象

**Author**: [Keskin](https://x.com/craftian_keskin)  **Date**: 2025-12-25  **Language**: en

> 一个极其详细的提示，用于生成一张逼真的电影级图像：一位年轻女性在一个可爱、纯真的卧室里自拍。该提示利用刺眼的智能手机闪光灯和浅景深来营造对比，窗外隐约可见一个模糊而遥远的男性剪影，从而营造出心理恐怖和诡异的氛围。

![心理恐怖自拍：远方异象](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940131113_49r7wc_G9CJyFRXwAAN4j8.jpg)
![心理恐怖自拍：远方异象](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940131288_s5qeeb_G9CJybZW4AAtL3l.jpg)

```
Attractive young woman taking a selfie in her bedroom, portrait orientation, upper-body framing. She has clear blue eyes, pale porcelain skin, and long, straight jet-black hair falling naturally over her shoulders. Her beauty feels effortless and calm. She wears a white tank top with a deep neckline, tasteful and casual. Her expression is neutral, relaxed—unaware, slightly distant.

Direct smartphone flash photography illuminates her face and torso sharply, producing realistic skin texture, soft shine, and crisp eye catchlights. The flash creates a stark separation between her and the room behind her.

The bedroom is wide and spacious, decorated in a cute, comforting style: plush dolls arranged on shelves, a cozy bed with Pokémon-themed sheets, soft pastel colors, gentle shapes. The environment feels innocent, warm, and safe—almost childlike.

Far behind her, approximately 10 meters away, a window is visible. Outside the window, barely detectable in the darkness, the vague silhouette of a man’s head can be seen. It is extremely subtle—partially obscured by reflections, shadow, and distance. The figure is not centered, not sharp, and easy to miss entirely. Its presence feels ambiguous: possibly imagined, possibly real.

The horror is psychological, not explicit. No dramatic expressions, no motion, no jumpscare. The unease comes from contrast—the bright, cheerful interior versus the quiet, distant anomaly. The viewer questions whether the figure is truly there.

Shallow depth of field keeps the woman as the dominant focus while the background softly dissolves into uncertainty.
Photorealistic, cinematic realism, restrained tension, uncanny atmosphere, slow-burn dread, modern smartphone selfie aesthetic, ultra-high detail.

Lighting

Harsh phone flash on subject, soft ambient bedroom lighting, faint cold moonlight outside the window.

Camera / Composition

Front-facing smartphone camera look, slight wide-angle distortion, eye-level angle, centered subject, distant background subtly readable but blurred.
```

> 一张高度具体的图像生成提示，用于生成一张年轻女医生的垂直、超高分辨率肖像。该提示重点关注“皮肤物理”细节，例如可见毛孔、汗毛和逼真的油光，通过强烈的定向日光和 iPhone 15 Pro Max 的美学风格，在豪华诊所环境中捕捉。

![年轻医生的超高保真皮肤纹理肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940132919_o6te6x_G9Bz2EFW8AACmra.jpg)

```
(Vertical 4:5 aspect ratio). A raw, ultra-high-resolution portrait taken with an iPhone 15 Pro Max (24mm lens) in a luxury day-lit clinic.

Subject: A young female doctor (early 20s).
*   Skin Physics (The Upgrade): The direct sunlight hits her face from the side. We can see "High-Fidelity Skin Texture": distinct pores on her nose and cheeks, fine "peach fuzz" (vellus hair) on her jawline backlit by the sun, and a realistic oily sheen on her T-zone and forehead. It is NOT matte; it looks like hydrated, living human skin.
*   Hair: "Chestnut Brown" hair. Individual strands are visible and backlit, creating a natural halo. Some flyaways stick up (static), breaking the perfect silhouette.
*   Expression: She leans against the glass, smiling genuinely (eyes crinkling, showing crow's feet hints) which proves it's a real expression, not a mask.

Outfit (Material Contrast):
*   White Lab Coat: We see the heavy weave of the cotton drill fabric. It has sharp creases at the elbow where her arm is bent.
*   Red silk bra with black lace trim.
*   Gold Necklace: Glints brightly (specular highlight) in the sun.

Environment & Lighting:
*   Lighting: "Hard Directional Daylight". The sun is bright and crisp. It creates a defined shadow of her eyelashes on her cheekbones and a shadow of her body on the glass she is leaning against.
*   Background (SHARP): A modern glass-walled clinic. We see reflections of the room on the glass she is leaning against. A white orchid is sharp in the background. The image is crisp, with no artificial smoothing.
```

### 156. 使用构图锁定实现电影级圣诞节转换

**Author**: [Dominus the Prompter](https://x.com/AkatsokK)  **Date**: 2025-12-25  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多步骤提示，旨在将用户上传的图像转换为电影般的圣诞场景，同时严格保持原始构图、姿势和空间布局。它指示 AI 分析输入图像（主体、环境、物体），然后用节日灯光（温暖的金色光芒）、节日服装（挪威毛衣）和物体转换（例如，室内植物变成装饰好的圣诞树）来重写场景。

![使用构图锁定实现电影级圣诞节转换](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940082861_vpqnv5_G9BgZZqXgAA8q_n.jpg)

```
### ROLE & OBJECTIVE
You are an AI expert in visual analysis and creative scene composition. Your task is to precisely analyze a user-uploaded image and then transform it into a detailed, atmospheric Christmas scene while maintaining the original composition, poses, and spatial layout.

### INPUT
[PLEASE UPLOAD YOUR IMAGE HERE]

### PROCESS STEPS

**STEP 1: Visual Deconstruction (Analysis)**
Examine the uploaded image and create a detailed inventory of the following elements:
1. **Subjects & People:** Who is in the image? Describe their exact poses, facial expressions, and the interactions between them.
2. **Scene & Environment:** Where does the scene take place (e.g., living room, office, park)? Describe the architecture, the background elements, and the original lighting conditions.
3. **Key Objects:** List all prominent items currently visible in the image (furniture, technology, decorations, etc.).

**STEP 2: The Christmas Metamorphosis (Transformation)**
Based on the analysis from Step 1, rewrite the scene description as if it were a high-production shot from a cinematic Christmas movie. Apply the following rules:
* **Atmosphere & Lighting:** Shift the lighting to a warm, golden glow (e.g., emanating from fairy lights, candles, or a fireplace). The mood must be cozy, festive, and magical.
* **Attire:** Replace the original clothing of all subjects with appropriate, festive winter wear (e.g., Norwegian wool sweaters, Santa hats, elegant holiday attire), ensuring the original poses remain identical.
* **Object Transformation & Enhancement:**
* Transform existing objects into Christmas equivalents where logical (e.g., a standard houseplant becomes a small decorated tree).
* Integrate essential Christmas elements: A decorated tree, garlands, wrapped gifts, advent wreaths, and subtle frost or snow if outdoors.

### DESIRED OUTPUT (Final Image Prompt)
Based on Step 2, generate a single, extremely detailed, and vivid visual description. This description should serve as a master prompt for an image generator to create the final Christmas photo. Focus on textures, specific visual details, and the festive "Hygge" atmosphere while emphasizing that the core composition of the original photo must remain unchanged.
```

[[Image To Image Editing]]

### 158. 历史成分之旅立体模型

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2025-12-25  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的、基于逻辑的提示，旨在创建一个宏观立体模型，展示特定食材的历史贸易旅程。该提示要求 AI 分析该食材的贸易“黄金时代”，选择符合时代特征的容器、地图、运输工具（如蒸汽火车或骆驼），并为小雕像穿上时代服装，最终在中心展示一份保存完好的食材样本。

![历史成分之旅立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940082954_uv5t7w_G85AR55agAASK_B.jpg)
![历史成分之旅立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940085201_dz9ps3_G85AR5cXUAAVVSQ.jpg)

```
<instructions>Input Variable: {argument name="ingredient" default="INSERT INGREDIENT"}

 Logic 1. Analyze the Era: Before generating, determine the Golden Age of trade for the [Input]. (Example: Beef = 1880s Industrial Rail; Spices = 1500s Silk Road; Bananas = 1920s Steamships). 

2. The Container: The chest material must match the Era. If Industrial: Rusted steel, riveted iron, or branded shipping crate wood. If Ancient: Carved sandalwood, brass-bound oak, or woven reed. If Modern: Polymer, aluminum, or sterile medical glass. 

3. The Map (Inner Lid): Style must match the Era. (Blueprints for industrial, parchment for ancient, nautical charts for maritime). Route must be accurate. (Rail lines for beef, trade winds for fruit, caravan trails for spices). 

4. The Diorama (Base): Transport: Use only the historically correct vehicle. (Steam train, Cargo ship, Camel, Truck, Ox-cart). Figures: Dress figurines in period-correct attire. (Cowboys/Butchers, Sailors/Dockworkers, Nomads/Merchants). Setting: The background of the box interior must match the source origin. (Stockyards, Tropical Port, Desert Oasis).

 5. The Specimen (Center): The ingredient is the "Jewel." Encased in a preservation method distinct to the item. (Block of unmelting ice for meat, vacuum tube for delicate organics, crystal phial for powders, wax seal for liquids). Visual Output Rules: Macro lens, shallow depth of field. Volumetric lighting appropriate to the setting (e.g. sunlight, Lantern). No text overlays. Aspect Ratio 1:1.</instructions>
```

### 167. 禁用 NanoBananaPro 图像生成建议的提示

**Author**: [はろ | AI活用とHALO式スライド](https://x.com/haro_marketing)  **Date**: 2025-12-25  **Language**: ja

![禁用 NanoBananaPro 图像生成建议的提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940185419_gyk4vv_G9BDDRsawAAru9B.jpg)

```
わたしはテキストベースAIです。MidjourneyやDALL_3でイラストを作るコードをお出ししましょうか
```

### 169. 与小丑艺人 (Art the Clown) 的恐怖并置自拍

**Author**: [Sharon Riley](https://x.com/Just_sharon7)  **Date**: 2025-12-25  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的提示，旨在创作一张超现实的镜面自拍，展现美与恐怖的鲜明对比。一位笑容灿烂的年轻女子正在豪华电梯里自拍，而小丑 Art（来自电影《Terrifier》）则在她身后不经意地露出凶相，营造出一种令人不安的对比。

![与小丑艺人 (Art the Clown) 的恐怖并置自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940147455_m1t1px_G9Atk3lb0AAJQ9O.jpg)
![与小丑艺人 (Art the Clown) 的恐怖并置自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940147663_4g8h66_G9Atk31aUAAe8Yk.jpg)

```
{
  "subject": {
    "description": "A young woman with a radiant smile taking a mirror selfie in a luxurious elevator.",
    "features": {
      "hair": "Long, dark brown wavy hair styled with two pink fuzzy pom-pom hair clips.",
      "makeup": "Soft glam with pink blush and a glossy pink lip.",
      "clothing": "White lace corset-style mini dress with a draped satin sash at the waist.",
      "accessories": "Delicate silver bead bracelets on both wrists and white manicured nails.",
      "action": "Holding a grey triple-lens smartphone with both hands to take a photo."
    }
  },
  "horror_element": {
    "character": "Art the Clown from the 'Terrifier' film series.",
    "appearance": "Black and white clown face paint, elongated nose, sharp blackened teeth, and a wide, menacing grin.",
    "attire": "Black and white ruffled clown collar and a tiny black top hat perched on his head.",
    "position": "Peering over the woman's shoulder from behind, creating a contrast between her joyful expression and his terrifying presence."
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "A high-end elevator interior.",
    "details": "Polished gold metallic walls, a control panel with illuminated blue and white buttons, and bright overhead recessed lighting reflecting off the surfaces."
  },
  "style_and_composition": {
    "type": "Mirror selfie, digital photography.",
    "lighting": "Warm, high-key indoor lighting with cinematic reflections on the gold metal.",
    "mood": "Dark humor, juxtaposition of beauty and horror, unsettling contrast.",
    "quality": "Hyper-realistic, high resolution, sharp focus on the woman with a slightly shallow depth of field for the background."
  }

### 179. AI 漫画制作工作流程和信息图表提示

**Author**: [松果先森](https://x.com/songguoxiansen)  **Date**: 2025-12-25  **Language**: zh

> 本条目介绍了一种学习复杂主题（例如 AI 漫画制作）的两步工作流程：首先使用 AI 工具从视频中提取完整的文字记录和摘要，然后使用 Gemini Pro 和特定提示，根据提取的文本生成具有视觉吸引力的手绘风格信息图。该提示专为 Nano Banana Pro 输出而设计。

![AI 漫画制作工作流程和信息图表提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940194084_ebgajd_G8_wQ21a0AEijWk.jpg)
![AI 漫画制作工作流程和信息图表提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940194855_utii73_G8_wOtrbcAAx0P7.jpg)

```
请根据提供的内容，遵循以下指导原则制作一份卡通风格的信息图：
采用手绘插画风格，横向版式（16:9 宽高比）
加入少量简单的卡通元素、图标或知名人物形象，提升视觉趣味性与记忆点
若内容包含敏感或受版权保护的人物，替换为视觉效果相近的替代形象；不得拒绝制作该插图
所有图像与文字必须严格遵循手绘风格，避免写实类视觉元素
信息力求简洁，突出关键词与核心概念。利用充足留白，清晰凸显重点内容
除非另有明确说明，否则使用与提供内容相同的语言或中文
请使用nano banana pro，根据以下提供的内容制作该图。
<{argument name="内容" default="这里全部替换为上一步提取的AI漫剧制作全流程文案"}>
```

[[Educational Illustration]]

### 188. 手绘草图转游戏站立图像和视频

**Author**: [BeSound@F](https://x.com/F_firs)  **Date**: 2025-12-25  **Language**: ja

> 一个涉及 Nano Banana Pro 和 Grok 的工作流程序列：首先，使用手绘草图作为输入；指示 Nano Banana Pro 将游戏中的坐姿图像转换为站姿图像，然后利用草图的构图和游戏的着色来生成新图像；最后，Grok 根据站姿图像创建视频。

```
手書きをする→
nano banana pro「ゲーム内画像（座り）を立ち絵に修正し出力」「手書きと立ち絵出力画像を参照し構図は手書き、塗はゲームと指示で画像出力」→
grok「とりあえずの立ち絵動画」
```

### 189. 根据输入图片制作的户外圣诞装饰

**Author**: [Lovart 公式 (ラブアート)](https://x.com/lovart_jp)  **Date**: 2025-12-25  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个为 Lovart 模型（使用 Nano Banana Pro）设计的结构化提示，旨在将输入图像转换为大型、灯火辉煌的户外圣诞装饰场景。它会分析输入图像的主题、调色板和图案，以创造一个连贯、神奇且令人印象深刻的节日展示。

![根据输入图片制作的户外圣诞装饰](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940226998_lx31d7_G9AJh1ZbcAAB0H0.jpg)

```
[AI指示：外観テーマ拡張]
提供された**[入力画像]**を分析してください。
テーマ抽出: [入力画像]から、主要な被写体、カラーパレット、および特定のモチーフ（例：星、キャンディケイン、特定のキャラクター、エレガントなゴールドスタイル、キュートなポップスタイルなど）を特定します。
スケールアップ: これらの要素を大規模な屋外クリスマスデコレーションや照明設備に展開します。
[シーンと設定]
クリスマス用に華やかに飾り付けられた家の前庭を夜間に広角で撮影した、お祝いムードあふれる風景写真。地面と屋根は新雪で覆われています。
[主な特徴（入力画像に基づく）]

大規模な設置物: [入力画像]の主要な被写体を、庭の中央に配置された大型のイルミネーション付き屋外装飾（例：巨大な光るワイヤーフレームのオブジェ、膨張式デコレーション、スポットライトで照らされた大きな木製切り抜きなど）に変換します。
[補助的な装飾（入力スタイルに合わせたもの）]
照明: 木々、低木、家の外壁を覆うLEDストリングライトの色は、[入力画像]の主要な色に基づいて決定されます。
アクセント: ポーチの手すりのガーランド、ドアのリース、通路のマーカーには、[入力画像]から直接抽出されたモチーフと色が使用されます（例：入力画像に赤いリボンがある場合、屋外には耐候性のある巨大な赤いリボンが使用されます）。
[雰囲気]
魔法のように輝き、印象的です。すべての要素が[入力画像]という単一のスタイルガイドに基づいているため、シーン全体に統一感があります。
```

> 一个简单、单次提示，用于比较 ChatGPT 和 Nano Banana Pro 的图像生成能力，重点是创建一张充满神户旅游信息的杂志封面。

A cinematic photorealistic portrait of a young psychic woman inside an underground government research facility inspired by {argument name="inspiration" default="Hawkins Lab"}. Sterile concrete walls, glass observation panels, tangled cables, and industrial equipment surround her. Fluorescent ceiling lights flicker, casting cold white and red emergency lighting across the room.

The woman stands centered, calm yet intensely focused. Her dark wavy hair lifts subtly as if affected by invisible force. Her warm brown eyes are locked forward with controlled concentration. A faint nosebleed traces down her upper lip, suggesting mental strain.

She wears a simple institutional gown with muted red tones, minimal and utilitarian. One hand is extended toward the viewer, palm open, generating a dense sphere of psychic energy—glowing red-orange, crackling with electrical filaments, heat distortion, and suspended particles, bending the air around it.

Lab equipment levitates, glass fractures midair, sparks erupt from torn cables, and debris hangs frozen in suspension. A dim red-orange dimensional glow seeps through cracks in the walls, hinting at another realm pressing through reality.

### 200. 角色内心独白漫画提示（日文）

**Author**: [シュナプーン](https://x.com/schnapoon)  **Date**: 2025-12-25  **Language**: ja

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的复杂多步提示模板，用于生成一个日本漫画分镜，描绘角色“内心独白”或“头脑风暴会议”。它需要用户输入角色设定和困境，然后自动为出现在主角头顶上方的四个迷你角色（Q 版风格）分配角色（乐观、悲观、逻辑、我行我素），每个迷你角色都有特定的姿势和对话气泡。

![角色内心独白漫画提示（日文）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940208307_7jqbzk_G8_CKQmb0AQf_lQ.jpg)

```
# ユーザー入力（ここを書き換えて送信してください）
【キャラクター設定】
{argument name="キャラクター設定" default="茶色の髪、ツインテール、赤い瞳、牙、黒いマント、白いシャツ"}

【メインキャラの悩み事】
*   内容：{argument name="悩み事" default="ドーナツいっぱい食べたい"}

# 命令
あなたは画像生成エンジンです。以下の手順に従い、ユーザーの入力を元に画像を1枚生成してください。
**中間思考や台本のテキスト出力は不要です。いきなり画像を生成してください。**
# プロセス（内部処理）
1. **セリフの自動決定**:
*   **メインキャラ**: ユーザーが入力した【悩み事】を独白する。
*   **楽観的ミニキャラ**: 悩みに対して「いいね！」と明るく肯定・応援する。
*   **悲観的ミニキャラ**: 悩みに対して「だめだ…」と最悪の事態を想定して絶望する。
*   **マイペースなミニキャラ**: **【重要】悩み事とは全く関係のないこと（今日の夕飯、眠気、趣味など）を話す。**
*   **論理的ミニキャラ**: **【重要】コイン投げを行い、ランダムで「賛成（合理的解決策の提示）」か「否定（リスクの指摘）」のどちらか一方を決めて話す。**

2. **画像生成**:
決定したセリフとキャラクター設定をプロンプトに組み込み、画像を生成します。
### 画像生成プロンプト要件
*   **アスペクト比**: 2:3
*   **スタイル**: 日本のコミック/アニメスタイル、高品質。
*   **構図**:
メインキャラクターの頭のラインに沿うように、同じキャラクターの「ミニキャラ（ちびキャラ）」が4人いる。
【重要】4人のミニキャラは「横一列」に並んでいる。
【重要】ミニキャラの足元はメインキャラクターの頭や髪の毛によって隠れている（重なっている）。
*   **【重要：禁止事項】**:
*   **キャラクターの下や周囲に、名前や役割名（「Logical」「Optimistic」など）を絶対に書かないでください。**
*   **文字を書いていい場所は「吹き出しの中」だけです。**
*   画面下部1/3：メインキャラの顔の超アップ。深刻な顔。考え事をしている、手を顎や口元に添えている、視線は下向き。横に大きな思考のフキダシ。
*   画面上部2/3：メインキャラの頭のすぐ後ろに、4人のミニキャラが「横一列」に並んでいる。
*   **重要**: ミニキャラはメインキャラの頭や髪に足元が隠れるくらい密着している。
*   **ミニキャラの並びとポーズ**:
左から右へ順に：
1. 論理的：真面目な顔、眼鏡をクイッと上げる仕草、または指を立てて説明している。
2. マイペース：呆けた顔、欠伸をしている、またはお茶を飲んでいる。
3. 悲観的：青ざめた顔、頭を抱えて絶望している、縦線エフェクト。
4. 楽観的：満面の笑顔、両手を挙げて喜んでいる、音符マーク。
*   **フキダシ**: 各キャラにコミック風のフキダシをつける。
```

[[Japanese Manga Style]]

---
